خاتمة ) لمباحث العقول ( في الجن والشياطين فإنها أيضا من الجواهر الغائية عن حواسنا ( وهي عند المليين أجسام تتشكل بأني شكل شاءت ) وتقدر على أن تتولج في بواطن الحيوانات وتنفذ في منافذها الضيقة نفوذ الهواء المستنشق واختلفوا في اختلافهما بالنوع مع الاتفاق على أنهما من أصناف المكلفين كالملك والأنس ) ومنعه الفلاسفة لأنها إما أن تكون ) الأجسام ( طليقة أو لا، وكلاهما باطل، أما الأول فلأنه يلزم أن لا تقدر ) هي ) على الأفعال الشاقة وتتلاشى بأدنى قوة وسبب من خارج يصل إليهما ( وهو خلاف ما يعتقدونه، وأما الثاني : فلانه يوجب أن ترى ولو جوزنا أجساما كثيفة لا نراها لجاز أن يكون بحضرتنا جبال وبلاد لا نراها وبوقات وطبول نسمعها وهو سفسطة ) محضة ) والجواب : أن لطفها بمعنى الشفافية ) أي عدم اللون ( فلا يلزم أحد الأمرين لجواز أن يقوى الشفاف ( الذي لا لون له ) على الأفعال الشاقة ولا ينفعل بسرعة فلا نراها وبالجملة فإن أردتم باللطافة الشفافية فتختار أنها لطيفة ولا يلزم عدم قوتها على تلك الأفعال ( وإن أردتم بها ) سرعة الانفعال والانقسام إلى أجزاء ) متصغرة ( ورقة القوم ) فإن اللطافة تطلق على هذه المعاني ( فتختار أنها غير لطيفة ولا يلزم رؤيتها كالسماء ) إلا أنه يشكل سهولة تشكلها بأي شكل شاءت، فلذلك قال : ( كيف وقد يفيض عليها القادر المختار مع لطافتها ( ورقتها (قوة عظيمة فإن القوة لا تتعلق بالقوام) في الرقة والغلظ لا باحثة في الصغر والكبر ) ألا ترى أن قوام الإنسان دون قوام الحديد والحجر ، وترى بعضهم يقتل الحديد ويكسر الحجر ويصدر منه ما لا يمكن أن يسد إلى غلظ القوام وترى الحيوانات مختلفة في القوة اختلافاً ليس بحسب اختلاف القوام والجثة ( كما في الأسد مع الحمار .
Conclusion for the discussions of the intellects on jinn and devils: they are also among the substances hidden from our senses. They are, according to the adherents of the religions, bodies that can take any form they wish, and they are able to enter into the interiors of animals and penetrate their narrow orifices like the passage of inhaled air. They differed as to whether they differ in species, while agreeing that they are among the types of responsible beings like angels and humans. The philosophers rejected this because [the bodies] are either Lā'iqah (loose/sublime) or not, and both are invalid. As for the first, it would entail that they cannot perform strenuous actions and would disintegrate with the slightest force from outside reaching them, contrary to what they believe. As for the second, it would require that they be visible; if we allow dense bodies we do not see, it would be possible that there are mountains and countries present with us that we do not see, and horns and drums we hear, which is pure sophistry. The answer: Their subtlety means transparency, i.e., absence of color, so neither consequence follows because it is possible for a transparent [body] which has no color to have strength for strenuous actions and not be affected quickly, so we do not see them. In summary: If by 'subtlety' you mean transparency, then we choose that they are subtle and it does not entail lack of strength for those actions. And if by it you mean quick susceptibility and division into small parts and thinness of substance, for 'subtlety' is used for these meanings, then we choose that they are not subtle, and it does not entail they are visible, like the sky. However, the ease of their taking any shape is problematic, therefore he said: 'How? For the Omnipotent Chosen bestows upon them, despite their subtlety and thinness, great power, for power is not related to bodily constitution in thinness or thickness, nor restricted to smallness or largeness. Do you not see that the constitution of man is weaker than that of iron and stone, yet you see some of them kill iron and break stone and produce what cannot be attributed to thickness of constitution? And you see animals differing in strength not according to their constitution and body, like the lion with the donkey.'
Source pages p. 266

Commentary
This passage is a discussion on jinn and devils, concluding the section on intellects. It first states that jinn and devils are substances hidden from our senses, and according to religious people, they are bodies that can take any shape and enter narrow places. Then it presents the philosophers' objection: either these bodies are subtle (لطيفة) or not. If subtle, they would be too weak for strenuous actions. If not subtle, they would be visible, and if we allow invisible dense bodies, it would lead to sophistry. The answer distinguishes two meanings of 'subtle': (1) transparency (الشفافية), i.e., having no color; in this sense, they are subtle, and transparency does not prevent strength. (2) quick susceptibility and divisibility; in this sense, they are not subtle, but they are not necessarily visible (like the sky). The author then notes the problem of them taking any shape and gives a final point: God can give them great power regardless of bodily constitution, as seen in the strength of animals.

Key Terms
الجن
الشياطين
اللطافة
الشفافية
السفسطة

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: Subtlety (لطافة) always implies weakness and fragility, so invisible bodies cannot be strong.
Correction: The author shows that subtlety can mean transparency, which does not preclude strength. Thus, jinn can be both invisible and powerful.

Checkpoint
According to the author, which meaning of 'subtlety' (اللطافة) avoids the philosophers' objection that jinn would be weak?
A) Quick susceptibility to change
B) Transparency (absence of color)
C) Thinness of substance
D) Divisibility into small parts

Key Takeaway
Jinn are invisible not because they are weak, but because they are transparent, and God can give them strength regardless of their bodily constitution.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
The philosophers rejected jinn because they could not be perceived. Are there areas in your own life where you only believe what you can see or sense? How does this passage challenge that tendency, and what unseen realities are you called to affirm today?
?
The author argues that God can grant power to subtle bodies. Do you truly trust that God's power is not limited by natural laws? What impossible situation are you facing right now where you need to believe that God can override apparent weaknesses?
?
This lesson distinguishes two meanings of 'subtlety' to resolve a confusion. How often do you miss the truth because you assume a word has only one meaning? Is there a verse of the Quran or a teaching of the Prophet (peace be upon him) that you might have misunderstood because of such an assumption? Commit today to re-examine it with a fresh reading.

Jinn and Devils as Earthly Souls
Presentation of the first opinion: jinn and devils are earthly souls.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand the first opinion that identifies jinn and devils as earthly souls, including the classification of souls and the rejection of the variant reading.

Core Idea
Some scholars identified jinn and devils as earthly souls managing the elements.

This lesson explores the first opinion presented by the author on the nature of jinn and devils. According to this view, souls that manage the celestial spheres are celestial, while those managing the elements are earthly. Among these earthly souls are earthly angels, jinn, and devils. The passage also addresses a variant reading that incorrectly identifies these entities as archangels.

Guided Path
1
Read the passage carefully
Read the Arabic passage for the first opinion once to get an overview. Then read the translation.
Notice the classification of souls.
2
Understand the classification of souls
Identify the two categories: celestial souls (managing celestial bodies) and earthly souls (managing elements).
This distinction is key.
3
Note the diversity of earthly souls
List the types: earthly angels, jinn, devils. The Prophet mentioned angels of mountains, rains, seas.
4
Examine the variant reading
Some copies have 'karbiyya' instead of 'earthly'. The passage explains why this is not suitable because archangels are absorbed in divine majesty.
This rejection reinforces the first opinion.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
قال قوم: هي النفوس الأرضية ) فإن النفس إن كانت مدبرة للأجرام العلوية فهي النفس الفلكية، وإن كانت مديرة للعناصر فهي النفس الأرضية أي السفلية (وهي مختلفة فمنها الملائكة الأرضية وإليها أشار عليه السلام بقوله : ( أتاني ملك الجبال وملك الأمطار وملك البحار، وقد وقع في بعض النسخ بدل الأرضية الكروبية بتخفيف الراء أي الملائكة المقربون ورد بأنه غير مناسب لأن الكروبية من الملائكة هم المهيمون المستغرقون أنوار جلال الله سبحانه وتعالى بحيث لا يتفرغون معه لشيء أصلاً لا لتدبير الأجسام ولا للتأثير فيها ( ومنها الجن ومنها الشياطين وغير ذلك فهذه جنود لربك لا يعلمها إلا هو، وقال قوم: هي النفوس الناطقة المفارقة فالخيرة) من المفارقة عن الأبدان ( تتعلق بالخيرة من المقارنة لها نوعاً من التعلق (وتعاونها على الخير) والسداد ( وهي الجن والشريرة ( منها ( تتعلق بالشريرة وتعاونها على الشر والفساد ) وهي الشياطين والله أعلم بحقائق الأمور ) .
تم الجزء السابع ويليه الجزء الثامن وأوله الموقف الخامس في الإلهيات
Some people said: They are the earthly souls. For if the soul is a manager of the celestial bodies, it is the celestial soul, and if it is a manager of the elements, it is the earthly soul, i.e., the lower soul. They are diverse: among them are the earthly angels, and the Prophet (peace be upon him) alluded to them in his saying: 'The angel of mountains came to me, the angel of rains, and the angel of seas.' And in some copies, instead of 'earthly,' it is 'karbiyya' (with a lightened rā'), i.e., the archangels. It was objected that this is inappropriate because the karbiyya are the absorbed angels who are overwhelmed by the lights of the majesty of Allah, such that they do not engage with anything at all, not even with the management of bodies or their influence. And among them are jinn and devils and others; these are the armies of your Lord, none knows them but Him. And some said: They are the separated discursive souls. The good ones among those separated from bodies attach to the good ones among those associated [with bodies] in some kind of attachment and cooperate with them in goodness and rightness, and they are the jinn. And the evil ones among them attach to the evil ones and cooperate with them in evil and corruption, and they are the devils. And Allah knows best the realities of things. The seventh part ends, followed by the eighth part, beginning with the Fifth Standpoint on the Divine Matters.
Source pages p. 267

Commentary
This passage presents two opinions about jinn and devils. The first opinion identifies them with earthly souls (النفوس الأرضية), which are those that manage the elements rather than the celestial spheres. These include earthly angels, jinn, and devils. A variant reading replaces 'earthly' with 'karbiyya' (archangels), but this is rejected because archangels are absorbed in divine glory and do not engage in material management. The second opinion identifies them with separated rational souls (النفوس الناطقة المفارقة), where good souls cooperate with good associated souls (jinn) and evil souls cooperate with evil associated souls (devils). The passage ends with the colophon of the volume.

Key Terms
النفوس الأرضية
النفوس الفلكية
الملائكة الأرضية
الكروبية

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: Some might think jinn and devils are completely different from souls, but this opinion identifies them as types of earthly souls.
Correction: The passage clearly includes jinn and devils among earthly souls, which are a category of souls managing the elements.

Checkpoint
According to the first opinion, which of the following is NOT included among earthly souls?
A) Earthly angels
B) Jinn
C) Devils
D) Archangels (karbiyya)

Key Takeaway
The first opinion identifies jinn and devils as earthly souls, distinct from celestial souls, and rejects the variant reading that would make them archangels.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
The passage mentions that the karbiyya are so absorbed in Allah's majesty that they cannot engage in any management or influence of bodies. How absorbed are you in your daily affairs, and what would it take for you to become more absorbed in the awareness of Allah's majesty? Will you commit to a specific daily practice to increase that awareness?
?
The Prophet (peace be upon him) spoke of specific angels managing mountains, rains, and seas. Have you ever recognized Allah's control over nature through these angels? The next time you see rain or a mountain, will you consciously remember that Allah has appointed angels for these tasks, and thank Him for His detailed care?
?
This opinion classifies jinn and devils as 'earthly souls' — lower souls managing the elements. Does this classification change how you perceive the unseen world? Are you ready to treat the reality of jinn and devils with the seriousness it deserves, knowing they manage aspects of your environment? What is one concrete action you will take today to seek protection from their harm or to believe more firmly in their existence?

Jinn and Devils as Separated Discursive Souls
Presentation of the second opinion: jinn and devils are separated discursive souls.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand the second opinion that identifies jinn and devils as separated rational souls, with good souls becoming jinn and evil souls becoming devils.

Core Idea
Another opinion held that jinn are good separated souls and devils are evil separated souls.

This lesson covers the second opinion introduced by the author, which views jinn and devils as separated discursive souls. According to this view, when souls separate from bodies, good ones cooperate with good people and are called jinn, while evil ones cooperate with evil people and are called devils.

Guided Path
1
Read the passage for the second opinion
Read the Arabic and translation for the second opinion. Notice the key terms.
2
Understand the concept of separated souls
Separated discursive souls are rational souls that have left the body. They can still attach to living souls.
This is a different category from earthly souls.
3
Distinguish good and evil souls
The passage divides them: good souls attach to good people and cooperate in goodness; these are jinn. Evil souls attach to evil people and cooperate in evil; these are devils.
4
Note the cooperation aspect
The cooperation is a type of attachment (تعلق) and mutual assistance. This explains how jinn and devils interact with humans.
The text says 'تعاونها على الخير' and 'تعاونها على الشر'.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books

A) Earthly souls

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
If good and evil souls seek out and cooperate with humans of like nature, what kind of spirits are you attracting through your daily thoughts and actions? Are you comfortable with the answer?
?
This opinion remains uncertain ('Allah knows best'). Does your faith depend on knowing the exact nature of jinn and devils, or can you submit to Allah's knowledge while examining your own soul's attachment to good or evil?
?
Since the passage suggests that separated souls cooperate with embodied souls, how actively are you seeking the cooperation of good spirits in your pursuit of righteousness? What one change could you make today to invite that cooperation?
